166.8(1): gtan tshigs yin/ blta ba'i rnam grangs brjod las 'das/ rtsal stobs blo dang 
166.9(1): rig pa'i kha bsgyur yin/ 'khor 'das gnyis med 'dres nas zil gyis mnan pa'o/ /
166.10(1): de nyid a ti mu wer nyid/ yang dag don gyi khyad par 'phags/ theg brgyad 'dzin 
166.11(1): pa zil gyis mnan/ rtag chad gnyis kyi bdud dpung 'joms/ nga bdag 'dzin

166.14(1): par bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //
166.15(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa/ bon nyid don gyi lta ba de lags na/ de don

166.17(1): la gsungs pa/ gnas lugs bon nyid mtha' dang bral/ de don rgyud la sbyar ba 
166.18(1): na/ snang ba phyi yi 'dzin pa bcad/ rig shes nang gi 'gyu ba bzung / a ti mu wer 
166.19(1): ngang nyid la/ dbyer med dbyings su bsgom pa'o/ /yang dag don la sgom 'dod 
166.20(1): rig pa phyi yi spros mtha' bcad/ 'gyu ba nang gi 'dzin pa btang / a ti mu 
166.21(1): wer mkha' khyab du/ rang shar ngos bzung dbyer med du/ ma bcos ngang la rig pa 
167.1(1): bzhag /snang ba'i rjes mi 'breng / 'ong ba'i mdun mi bsdud/ rang sar bzhag pa 
167.2(1): bsgom par bya/ de la bdag 'dzin zhan nas bsgom pa'i bdud/ gang yang skyon du

167.5(1): la gnas pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /rig pa rten dang bral ba'i ngo bo yin/ ma yengs rig

167.7(1): ni gong nas gong du bogs 'byin te/ 'dzin med lhug par gnas na 'khor 'das

167.9(1): bdud 'dul rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ bsgom pa bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o/ //
167.10(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyi zhus pa/ a ti mu wer bsgom pa de lags na/ yang dag 
167.11(1): bon nyid 'bras bu thob tshul ci ltar lags/ zhes zhus pas/ dbal chen khro bo'i 
167.12(1): bka' stsal pa/ nyon cig 'khor 'dus thams cad kun/ bon nyid 'bras bu'i thob 
167.13(1): tshul ni/ rnam pa gnyis ni bshad par bya/ gnas skabs dang ni mthar thug go /
167.14(1): gnas skabs 'bras bu rnam pa dgu/ theg pa'i sgo nas thob tshul yin/ bogs thon 
167.15(1): nyams dang rtsal rnyed nas/ sems shes rdzogs sku'i zhal mthong dang / rang sems

167.17(1): 'bras bu yin/ mthar thug don gyi 'bras bu ni/ a ti mu wer mngon 'gyur te/

167.21(1): yin pas/ khyad 'phags a ti mu wer du/ rig pa'i snying po bon sku rdzogs/ bdag

168.4(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// //
168.5(1): 7 de yi tshe de yi dus na/ thams cad bon nyid mthar thug rna ru dkar po'i

168.21(1): yang phyi yi gnas/ gangs dkar stag so bkram pa 'dra ba dang / g.ya' sngon 'brong

169.3(1): nags gnyan stag gzig 'khros pa 'dra ba dang / g.ya' spangs sman btsun chags

169.9(1): grib med par shes/ de dag nang gi gnas su bstan/ gsang ba'i gnas ni/ bdag 
169.10(1): gi nyams 'thad bar chod med par shes/ de dag gsang ba'i gnas su bstan/ de

169.17(1): gnas bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// //
169.18(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyi dgyes pa'i tshul gyis/ mchod pa mang po phul nas zhus

170.1(1): nyid ni/ mtshan dang ldan pa mtshan nyid tshul mi ldan/ phye na rnam pa gnyis su

171.1(1): khro bo'i 'bras bu 'di de la ster bar mi srid do/ /ces ge khod gsang ba'i rgyud las/
171.2(1): sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// //
171.3(1): 7 de nas yang dag bshad par bya/ bdud 'dul nga nyid bsgrub pa na/ rdzas

252.2(1): po rtsal nyid du/ bdud 'dul dbal gyi rol pas 'byung / nyon mongs bdud 'dul 
252.3(1): ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ sku dang ye shes kyi lha dang / las kyi lha yi dbye bsdu 
252.4(1): dgos ched bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// //
252.5(1): 7 de nas ku byi mang ke yis/ ston pa la zhus pa/ sku dang ye shes las kyi lha/
252.6(1): sems su sbyor na ci ltar sbyor/ rol par bsgrub na ci ltar bsgrubs/ de yi don dang 
252.7(1): mngon tshig zhu/ gsol pa gsan dang bka' stsal pa/ e ma ho/ gab sbas gsang 
252.8(1): tshig mngon mthong dka'/ bdud 'dul ge khod rgyal po des/ sku gsum ye shes cho 
252.9(1): 'phrul yin/ de nyid rig pa sems su sbyar/ thig le nyag gcig snying por bsgrub/ nga 
252.10(1): bdag bdud bzhi 'joms pa'i dbal/ ge khod sku lnga lhun la rdzogs/ rtogs pas 
252.11(1): dgra bo dbyings su bsdus/ bdud 'dul sgrub pa'i 'bras bu yin/ khams gsum 
252.12(1): thams cad dus cig bsgral/ thugs rje bsgral ba'i dbal chen yin/ de yi thugs 
252.13(1): rje rol pa ste/ nga bdag 'joms pa'i dbal chen te/ phyi snod 'jig rten gsas 
252.14(1): mkhar brgyan/ nang bcud rol pa'i bdud 'dul sku/ gtso 'khor sprul pa'i lha 
252.15(1): tshogs rnams/ ri brag nags tshal ci snang shar/ ye shes rol pa'i sgrub lugs so/ /
252.16(1): don ni gdul bya gnyis snang ba/ zhi khro thugs rje gnyis snang gis/ gang la 'tshams 
252.17(1): pa'i ngos nas su/ bdud 'dul thabs bstan pa'o/ /gtan tshigs bon nyid gzhir 
252.18(1): bzhag nas/ bden pa gnyis kyi 'khrul lam bzlog /ngang nas zhi ba'i rnams la 
252.19(1): yang / bon nyid ye shes zhi dul te/ gdug pa bdud srin log pa la/ thugs rje khro 
252.20(1): bo'i cha lugs bstan/ bon nyid dbyings la ye shes shar/ gtan tshigs dbyings 
252.21(1): la thugs rje shar ba'i don/ thig le gcig la thabs shes 'byung / zhes gsungs te/
253.1(1): nyon mongs bdud 'dul ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ ge khod sems nyid sbyar te 
253.2(1): sgrub pa dang / gdul bya rol par bsgrubs pa dang / de'i don dang gtan tshigs 
253.3(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o/ / //
253.4(1): 7 de nas 'khor gyis zhus pa/ ge khod sems nyid bsgrub pa dang / de'i sgrub 
253.5(1): lugs la/ thabs dang rol pa ci ltar bgyis/ zhus pas/ bka' bstsal pa/ e ma ho/
253.6(1): ngo mtshar mgon po gsum gyi sku/ de la thugs rje ma 'gag shar/ sems nyid rol 
253.7(1): pa'i shar tshul yin/ de'i don la thag bcad pas/ ge khod sems su mnyam par 
253.8(1): gnas/ gsungs pa las/ ku byi mang kes phyi rabs don du zhus pa/ mgon po rnam 
253.9(1): gsum sems nyid lags na/ gzhi lam 'bras bu la rten mtshal lam mi mtshal zhus 
253.10(1): pas/ ston pa nyid kyis bka' bstsal pa/ ngo mtshar zhus pa'i don mthil du bshad 
253.11(1): kyi gus par nyon/ ye stong bon nyid spros mtha' bral/ dbyings kyi ngo bo bsgrub med 
253.12(1): na/ de don rgyud la ma 'byor phyir/ thugs rje shar tshul gnyis nas bstan/ don la 
253.13(1): thabs shes dbyer med yin/ gzhi dang lam dang 'bras bu gsum/ don la sbyar phyir 
253.14(1): yang dag 'tshal/ don nyid ma mthong bstan pa'i phyir/ tshig gi lo mas don tshol bas/
253.15(1): thabs tsam shes rab de la bstan/ dang po gzhi yi gnas tshul dang / ma rtogs 
253.16(1): 'khrul pa'i byung tshul dang / 'jug pa lam gyi bsgrod tshul dang / smin pa 'bras bu'i 
253.17(1): thob tshul dang / gzhi yi sems nyid don la sbyor/ dang po gzhi la gnyis yin te/
253.18(1): 'khrul pa'i gzhi dang ma 'khrul pa'o/ /'khrul pa'i gzhi la gnyis te/ 'khor ba 'khrul 
253.19(1): pa'i gzhi 'di ma rig pa las byung / mi 'khrul pa ni ye shes te/ de yi yin lugs ci 
253.20(1): tshugs kyang / yongs la khyab cing bdal pa dang / til gyi mar bzhin mnyam par 
253.21(1): gnas/ ris med chen por 'dug pa'o/ /'khrul las 'khor bar 'khyams lugs ni/
254.1(1): pha ma gnyis kyi sred len gyi/ rgyu rkyen dkar dmar sa bon las/ dug lnga phra rags 
254.2(1): 'khrul pa skyed/ dug lnga nyon mongs lnga 'dzin byas/ 'di 'deg gcod sogs sha 
254.3(1): khrag lus/ de la sdug bsngal chu bzhi 'khrug /'dzin pa yid kyi bya byed des/ rigs 
254.4(1): drug 'khor ba'i lam la sbyor/ nga bdag bzung 'dzin dam pos bcings/ 'khrul 
254.5(1): pa'i gzhi la 'khrul pa rten/ nyon mongs dug lnga skye 'phel byed/ ma rtogs 'khrul 
254.6(1): pa'i byung tshul lo/ /'jug pa lam gyi rim pa yang / lam dang lam min gnyis kyis 
254.7(1): bstan/ lam ma yin pa rnam pa gsum/ lam log lam med lam ltar snang / lam 
254.8(1): med byis pa skye bo la/ lam log mu stegs ge shan dun tse'i rigs/ lam tsam 'dzin 
254.9(1): pa rgyu bzhi spyod pa'o/ /lam dngos la yang rnam pa gsum gyis gtan la dbab/ rgyu 
254.10(1): lam du byed pa dang / 'bras bu lam du byed pa dang / 'jug rtsol bral ba gsum/
254.11(1): 'dir ni dbyer med gsang sngags lam/ 'bras bu'i lam byed pa'o/ /don nyid 
254.12(1): gsang sngags bsgyur lam bde rdzogs so/ /zhi khro'i thugs rje rol pa las/ 'byung lnga 
254.13(1): yab yum dbyer med du/ phung po lha dang dbyer med sbyar/ dgongs pa dbyer med 
254.14(1): 'bras bu la/ goms zhing 'dris par byed pa'i lam yang yin/ de la 'bras bu thob 
254.15(1): tshul yin/ lha dang dbyer med mthar skyol zhing / phung po lha ru grub pas na/ mthar 
254.16(1): phyin 'bras bu'i thob tshul yin/ nyon mongs dug 'joms ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud 
254.17(1): las/ ge khod sems dang dbyer med grub lugs dang / gzhi lam 'bras bu gtan 
254.18(1): la dbab pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// //
254.19(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa ni/ de ltar sems su bsgrub pa la/ sems kyi 
254.20(1): yin lugs ci ltar lags/ zhes zhus pas/ bka' stsal pa/ nyon cig 'khor kun 
254.21(1): legs pa ru/ snang srid 'khor 'das sems kyi rtsal/ thams cad khro bo'i rol pa 
255.1(1): yin/ sems las ma gtogs bon zhes med/ sems ni ye nas bon gyi dbyings/ ye 
255.2(1): shes lha sku ngo bo nyid/ de la ma 'gag longs sku las/ sna tshogs rol pa sprul pa'i 
255.3(1): sku/ de phyir gang shar sems su bstan/ de ltar sems su gnas pa la/ dbye ba med 
255.4(1): pa sngags kyi lam/ ge khod lha yi rol pa shar/ shar kyang sems nyid ngang la shar/
255.5(1): thim kyang sems nyid ngang du chub/ de ltar yin pa'i gtan tshigs kyang / sems 
255.6(1): nyid ma 'gag gsal la stong pa'i phyir/ shar ba nyid na rang bzhin stong / stong pa 
255.7(1): nyid la rang bzhin gsal/ dbye ba med pa'i ge khod sku/ de nyid sems kyi rang rtsal 
255.8(1): du/ dbye ba med pa bon nyid dbyings/ dbyer med sems kyi ngo bo la/ yod par mi 
255.9(1): bzung med kyang chal (phyal )bar stong pa ma yin pas/ sems nyid rtag chad mtha' 
255.10(1): dang bral/ gsal la ngos bzung med pa yi/ ngang la gnas pa a ti mu wer yin/
255.11(1): ces nyon mongs dug 'joms/ ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ sems kyi gnas 
255.12(1): lugs dang / sems su gtan la dbab pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// //
255.13(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa/ sems kyi yin lugs de lags na/ nyams su 
255.14(1): blang lugs ci ltar lags/ ces zhus pas/ bka' stsal pa/ de don du zhus pa shin 
255.15(1): tu legs/ sems nyid 'di ni kun la khyab/ rang bzhin bdal par yongs la gnas/
255.16(1): don du thig le nyag gcig yin/ sems nyid thig le nyag gcig la/ nyams su blang 
255.17(1): thabs bsam las 'das/ nyon mongs brgyad khri bzhi stong yang / sems las 'byung 
255.18(1): zhing sems kyi rtsal/ de dag gnyen po bon sgo ni/ brgyad khri bzhi stong bstan pa yang /
255.19(1): sems la byung zhing sems kyi rtsal/ de phyir sems la kun chub pa/ sems nyid snying 
255.20(1): po nyams su blang / sems la bltas pa rang shar bon/ ma lus rang rig dbyer med 
255.21(1): gsal/ a ti mu wer sku ru chub/ dngos med sems kyi rang rtsal las/ rol pa sku 
256.1(1): dang ye shes shar/ 'di nyid 'khor 'das 'byung ba'i gzhi/ 'khrul dang ma 'khrul 
256.2(1): gnyis yin no/ /de phyir sems nyid 'di la lta/ a ti mu wer sems su sgrub/ ge khod 
256.3(1): sems su ma shes na/ ye shes lha yang btsal bar dka'/ de phyir sems nyid nyams 
256.4(1): su blang / sems ni stong la ma 'gag pa/ gsal la ngos bzung med pa ru/ dbyer 
256.5(1): med ngang du gnas pa'i bon/ de ltar gnas na ge khod ni/ rang rig sems su rang 
256.6(1): bzhin shar/ bla med g.yung drung sa la phyin/ de yi 'bras bu de yin pas/ sems 
256.7(1): nyid nyams su lon par gyis/ phyi snod ge khod gzhal yas la/ nang bcud ge khod lha 
256.8(1): yi sku/ de dag 'dzin med sems su yang / ngang la gsal stong bsgom par bya/ de 
256.9(1): yang phyi ltar lha dang lha mo la/ nang ltar sems nyid rol pa ste/ gsang ba thig le 
256.10(1): nyag gcig yin/ thig le nyag gcig nyams su blang / ye nyid ston pa'i sku ru gyur/
256.11(1): bon sgo brgyad khri bzhi stong yang / rtsa ba sems kyi ngang du 'dus/ sna tshogs rol pa 
256.12(1): ci shar yang / ye shes tsam du ngo bo gcig /phyi nang snod bcud thams cad kyang / sku 
256.13(1): dang ye shes rol pa dang / gsas mkhar sems dang nyid du 'char/ de dag sems 
256.14(1): su 'ub chud pas/ thams cad sems su bsgom par bya/ sems ni dngos med rang 
256.15(1): gsal bas/ phyi dang nang dang dbye ba med/ rtag dang chad pas ma gos pas/ nyag 
256.16(1): gcig thig ler nyams su blang / ces nyon mongs dug 'joms ye shes 'khyil pa'i 
256.17(1): rgyud las/ sems nyid ci ltar nyams su blang lugs bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// //
256.18(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa/ ye nyid ston pa sangs rgyas sku/ ma 'gag 
256.19(1): rol pa'i thugs rje yis/ bon rnams gsungs pa ngo mtshar che/ sems nyams su len 
256.20(1): lugs de lags na/ sems dang bon nyid bsre lugs ci ltar lags/ de nyid so so 
256.21(1): lags sam gcig pa lags/ de bdag la ma 'tshal bshad par zhu/ ces zhus pas/
257.1(1): bka' stsal pa/ legs so nyon cig 'khor gyi tshogs/ sems dang bon nyid bsre 
257.2(1): lugs ni/ phyi nang gsang ba gsum du bstan/ phyi ltar shar ba'i snod bcud 'di/
257.3(1): sems kyi rol pa 'gag med rtsal/ rtag par 'dzin na bon nyid bsre lugs min/
257.4(1): shar tshul 'dzin med gnas pa ni/ sems dang bon nyid 'dres pa yin/ nang ltar 
257.5(1): sems su snang ba yi/ 'dzin pa tsam du ma 'gag pa/ ther zug phyogs cha ngar 'dzin 
257.6(1): bon ma yin/ gsal la ngos bzung med pa na/ sems dang bon nyid 'dres pa yin/
257.7(1): gsang ba sems nyid dngos med 'di/ ma 'gag ngang nas cir snang zhing / brtag 
257.8(1): na gang yang rang bzhin med/ de nyid bon dang dbyer med pas/ sems dang 
257.9(1): 'dres zhes brjod pa yin/ sems zhes tha snyad btags pa dang / bon nyid zhes su 
257.10(1): btags pa yang / kun rdzob mtshan ma tsam du so so ste/ don dam dbyings kyi ngang 
257.11(1): la tha dad med/ ci phyir bon sku sems kyi rol pa ste/ btags pa thams cad sems 
257.12(1): nyid do/ /yang dag don la bon dang sems/ so so ma yin gcig gi ngang / nyag 
257.13(1): gcig yin pas gcig gi dbyings/ 'khor 'das sems kyi rtsal du shar/ dbye bsdu 
257.14(1): med pas g.yung drung sku/ bla na med pa'i 'bras bu la/ don gyi sangs rgyas yin zhes 
257.15(1): brjod/ sems nyid thig le nyag gcig la/ 'khrul pas ngar 'dzin byas pa ni/ sdug 
257.16(1): bsngal chu bo rlabs ltar 'byung / 'dzin pas 'ching pa nga bdag yin/ phye na bon 
257.17(1): yang blo rtog sdug bsngal te/ mo gsham bu 'dod ci bzhin du/ rang rgyud sbyor bas 
257.18(1): lam yin pas/ dbyer med gsas mkhar don nyid ni/ rang rig sems la btsal 
257.19(1): bar bya/ tshig mtha' bcad na sems las 'das/ don du bsdu na nyag gcig sems/
257.20(1): dbyings su rtogs pa gcig chod yin/ mtha' bral bon nyid khyab bdal la/ bdag 
257.21(1): 'dzin spong ba ye nyid sku/ gcig dang du ma'i brjod pa bral/ 'khor ba myang 'das 
258.1(1): lam du bcad/ sdug bsngal bde ba'i dbyings su bsdu/ sems dang bon nyid gcig

258.5(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// //
258.6(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa/ rna ru dkar po khyad par gyi don ci ltar

258.9(1): khyad par yang rtse ston pa yin/ ye nyid ston pa'i sku ru rdzogs pa ni/ 'khor 'das

258.11(1): sngags dbyer med ston dus su/ khyad par don ston ci mi 'gal lam/ dbyer med 
258.12(1): lta ba ston dus su/ khyad par ston pa cang mi 'gal/ ces zhus pas/ bka' stsal pa/
258.13(1): ci phyir 'khor 'das bon sku sems/ phyi nang bon sku sems kyi rol pa ste/ sems kyi 
258.14(1): dbyings la che chung med/ brgyad khri bzhi stong sems la shar/ de phyir khyad par klong 
258.15(1): du kun grol bas/ khyad par lta ba ston pa ni/ che ba'i rtsal du shar ba ste/ dbyer med 
258.16(1): lam gyi bon 'byin yin/ yang dag bon la yang dag 'jug /ci phyir 'bras bu lam 
258.17(1): du byas pa'o/ /nged bshad bon 'di khyad par 'phags/ nam mkha' yang la nyi shar 
258.18(1): 'dra/ theg dgu khyad par lta ba grol/ yang rtse rna ru dkar po'i don/ ye nyid ston pa 
258.19(1): kun du bzang / gang yang ma spangs rgya ma chad/ mi spangs ma 'gag bsgrub bya bral/
258.20(1): mthar thug khyad par bon nyid yin/ 'khor bar ston pa ya mi nga / myang 'das ston 
258.21(1): pa yang nga yin te/ de phyir nga las ma byung bon med pas/ tshig tsam ngos nas phye ba 
259.1(1): las/ don la ngo bo gcig gi ngang / sdong po gcig la yal ga'i tshul/ yang rtse theg 
259.2(1): pa bon kun chub/ de phyir gsang 'dus bon bshad 'gal ba med/ ye nyid ston 
259.3(1): pa'i sku rdzogs pa/ ye dag lhun grub dri ma med/ gang gis ma bcos dgag sgrub bral/
259.4(1): ye nas sangs rgyas chen po la/ 'khor 'das gnyis ka'i bya sgrub rdzogs/ snang srid 
259.5(1): bon kun gang shar ba/ ye nyid ston pa'i klong la rdzogs/ ci'i phyir ye nas 'ub chud 
259.6(1): pas/ rdzogs ces bya ba'i gtan tshigs so/ /ye dag bon sku chen po la/ cir yang 
259.7(1): grub pa mi 'dug pas/ stong rdzogs ye sangs rgyas pa yin/ yang dag bon nyid ngang

259.11(1): rgyud las/ khyad par theg pa'i don bstan pa dang / bon thams cad ye nyid ston 
259.12(1): pa'i sku la rdzogs lugs kyi le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //
259.13(1): 7 de nas 'khor rnams kyis mchod pa phul te zhus pa/ khyad par bon gyi lta sgom 
259.14(1): 'bras bu'i don rnams bstan par 'tshal/ ye rdzogs don yang bshad par zhu/ zhes

259.20(1): ni/ nam mkha'i mtha' bzhin 'di yin med/ phyogs ris med pa'i bon du lta/ de 
259.21(1): nyid sgom pa dmigs gtad med/ rang so'i ngang la rjen ne sgom/ spyod pa blang dor 
260.1(1): bkag sgrub med/ shugs 'byung ngang la rang grol spyod/ 'bras bu'i don la re dogs 
260.2(1): med/ rtsol med rang la shar ba'i bon/ ye nyid ston pa'i sku ru rdzogs/ de lta bu'i 
260.3(1): don de la/ lta ba gdags su ming 'dogs bral/ 'di zhes su yis bstan du med/
260.4(1): de ltar de yi don nyid las/ sgom pa bya ru ci yang med/ ma yengs tsam du bzhag du 
260.5(1): yod/ spyod pa spyod bya'i yul las 'das/ rang kar ma yin rang grol bzhag /'bras 
260.6(1): bu gang yang bsgrub rgyu med/ gang shar dngos grub rol par bsdu/ de ltar khyad par 
260.7(1): don la dems chud nas/ dug lnga ma spangs sku lnga shar/ nyon mongs ye shes 'od du 
260.8(1): 'khyil/ dug gsum mgon po gsum du sgrol/ 'khor ba mya ngan 'das par rdzogs/
260.9(1): ye rdzogs g.yung drung yin pa'i phyir/ ye nyid ston pa kun tu bzang / nga yis bshad 
260.10(1): pa'i bon 'di la/ nyon mongs ye shes rang shar bas/ ma yengs sems kyi blta bar 
260.11(1): gyis/ skal ldan gshen gyis ltas pa yi/ nyon mongs ma spangs ye shes ngang / gsal 
260.12(1): la sgrib med ngang la gnas/ ye shes su yang mi 'dzin pa/ sal le hrig ge 'od du 
260.13(1): 'khyil/ de la ma yengs ngang gis ni/ dug lnga rang grol byas pa de/ ye nyid sku ru 
260.14(1): rdzogs ces bya/ nyon mongs bdud 'joms ye shes 'khyil pa'i rgyud las/ khyad par 
260.15(1): lta sgom dang ye rdzogs kyi don bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// /
260.16(1): 7 de nas yang 'khor gyis zhus pa/ bon sku'i ngang las rdzogs skur bstan/ gang 
260.17(1): zag ma rtogs pa rnams la/ nyon mongs ma spangs rang grol don bstan 'tshal/

260.19(1): bdag cag 'khor rnams la/ nyon mongs ma spangs rang grol don bstan 'tshal/

260.21(1): nyid myang 'das te/ ma spangs gnas su dag pa'i phyir/ nyon mongs lnga nyid ye shes 
261.1(1): yin/ ye shes tsam du shar ba yang / 'dzin pa med pa'i 'od zer tsam/ dug lnga shar 
261.2(1): tshad brtag na stong / stong zhes phyal bar mi gnas pas/ ma 'gag gsal la ljen ne 
261.3(1): ba/ rang 'byung ye shes ngang la gsal/ 'di ltar rig pa rang gsal 'di/ de nas 
261.4(1): bon sku ye dag yin/ de nas gzhan du btsal mi dgos/ hrig ge rang lugs so ma 
261.5(1): la/ bkag sgrub bya brtsal ming 'dogs bral/ nyon mongs ma spangs rang sar grol/
261.6(1): gti mug gsal ba'i ye shes te/ zhe sdang byams pa'i ye shes la/ 'phrag dog yangs 
261.7(1): pa'i ye shes te/ 'dod chags sbyin pa'i ye shes yin/ nga rgyal zhi ba'i ye shes so/ /

261.9(1): sgrub spang len med/ 'di ltar khyad par bsgrub bya med/ bkag sgrub bral ba'i bon 
261.10(1): nyid la/ ma spangs pa ni sangs rgyas yin/ rna ru dkar po dbyings kyi gnas/ 'jig 
261.11(1): 'bral med pa'i gsas mkhar yin/ bsgrub du rang la ye nas yod/ spang du gang
